CANDIDATE 2
generation_source: llm_sql_direct (label: llm_sql_direct)
raw_model_response: SELECT AVG(match_count) AS average_matches_per_season
FROM (
    SELECT s.season_id, COUNT(m.match_id) AS match_count
    FROM seasons s
    JOIN matches m ON s.season_id = m.season_id
    WHERE s.season_status = 'active'
    GROUP BY s.season_id
)
extracted_sql:
SELECT AVG(match_count) AS average_matches_per_season
FROM (
    SELECT s.season_id, COUNT(m.match_id) AS match_count
    FROM seasons s
    JOIN matches m ON s.season_id = m.season_id
    WHERE s.season_status = 'active'
    GROUP BY s.season_id
)
normalized_sql:
SELECT AVG(match_count) AS average_matches_per_season

    WHERE s.season_status = 'active'
    GROUP BY s.season_id
)

raw_model_response: SELECT AVG(match_count) AS average_matches_per_season
FROM (
    SELECT s.season_id, COUNT(m.match_id) AS match_count
    FROM seasons s
    JOIN matches m ON s.season_id = m.season_id
    GROUP BY s.season_id
    HAVING s.season_id IN (
        SELECT season_id
        FROM seasons
        WHERE season_status = 'active'
    )
) AS subquery;
